/* Automatic swiping */
.swiper-container {
  position: relative;
}

.swiper-container:hover .swiperButtonNext,
.swiper-container:hover .swiperButtonPrev {
  display: none;
}

.swiper-container:hover .swiper-pagination-bullet {
  opacity: 0
}
.swiper-container:hover .swiper-pagination-bullet-active {
  opacity: 1;
}

.swiper-container.autoplaying .swiperButtonNext,
.swiper-container.autoplaying .swiperButtonPrev {
  display: none;
}

.swiper-container.autoplaying .swiper-pagination-bullet {
  opacity: 0.5;
}

.swiper-container.autoplaying .swiper-pagination-bullet-active {
  opacity: 1;
}

.swiper-container .swiper-pagination-bullet {
  transition: opacity 0.3s;
}

.swiper-container.autoplaying .swiper-pagination-bullet {
  pointer-events: none;
}

.swiper-container.autoplaying .swiper-pagination-bullet-active {
  pointer-events: auto;
}

.swiper-container.autoplaying .swiper-pagination-bullet-active.swiper-pagination-bullet {
  opacity: 1;
}

.swiper-container.autoplaying .swiper-pagination-bullet-active.swiper-pagination-bullet:hover {
  opacity: 1;
}

.swiper-container.autoplaying .swiper-pagination-bullet-active.swiper-pagination-bullet:focus {
  opacity: 1;
}

  opacity: 1;
}

.swiper-container .swiper-pagination-bullet {

}

.swiper-container.autoplaying .swiper-pagination-bullet {
  pointer-events: none;
}

.swiper-container.autoplaying .swiper-pagination-bullet-active {
  pointer-events: auto;
}

  opacity: 1;
}

  opacity: 1;
}

  opacity: 1;
}

import { useEffect, useRef } from 'react';
import SwiperCore, { Autoplay, Navigation, Pagination } from 'swiper';
import { Swiper, SwiperSlide } from 'swiper/react';
import 'swiper/swiper-bundle.min.css';
import styles from '../styles/Testimonial.module.css';
import Image from 'next/image';
import profileImage from '../assets/images/testimonial_image.jpg';
import profileImage1 from '../assets/images/testimonial1_image.jpg';
import profileImage2 from '../assets/images/testimonial2_image.jpg';

SwiperCore.use([Autoplay, Navigation, Pagination]);

const Testimonial = () => {
  const swiperRef = useRef(null);

  useEffect(() => {
    const swiperInstance = swiperRef.current.swiper;
    if (swiperInstance) {
      swiperInstance.autoplay.start();
    }
    return () => {
      if (swiperInstance) {
        swiperInstance.autoplay.stop();
      }
    };
  }, []);

  return (
    <section className={styles.container}>
      <div className={`${styles.testimonial} ${styles.mySwiper}`}>
        <Swiper
          ref={swiperRef}
          spaceBetween={30}
          slidesPerView={1}
          navigation={{
            nextEl: `.${styles.swiperButtonNext}`,
            prevEl: `.${styles.swiperButtonPrev}`,
          }}
          pagination={{ clickable: true }}
          autoplay={{ delay: 5000 }}
        >
          <SwiperSlide className={styles.slide}>
            <Image src={profileImage} alt="" className={styles.image} />
            <p>
              Lorem ipsum dolor sit amet, consectetur adipisicing elit. Aperiam, saepe provident dolorem a quaerat quo
              error facere nihil deleniti eligendi ipsum adipisci, fugit, architecto amet asperiores doloremque deserunt
              eum nemo.
            </p>
            <i className={`${styles.quoteIcon} bx bxs-quote-alt-left`}></i>
            <div className={styles.details}>
              <span className={styles.name}>Marnie Lotter</span>
              <span className={styles.job}>Web Developer</span>
            </div>
          </SwiperSlide>
          <SwiperSlide className={styles.slide}>
            <Image src={profileImage1} alt="" className={styles.image} />
            <p>
              Lorem ipsum dolor sit amet, consectetur adipisicing elit. Aperiam, saepe provident dolorem a quaerat quo
              error facere nihil deleniti eligendi ipsum adipisci, fugit, architecto amet asperiores doloremque deserunt
              eum nemo.
            </p>
            <i className={`${styles.quoteIcon} bx bxs-quote-alt-left`}></i>
            <div className={styles.details}>
              <span className={styles.name}>Marnie Lotter</span>
              <span className={styles.job}>Web Developer</span>
            </div>
          </SwiperSlide>
          <SwiperSlide className={styles.slide}>
            <Image src={profileImage2} alt="" className={styles.image} />
            <p>
              Lorem ipsum dolor sit amet, consectetur adipisicing elit. Aperiam, saepe provident dolorem a quaerat quo
              error facere nihil deleniti eligendi ipsum adipisci, fugit, architecto amet asperiores doloremque deserunt
              eum nemo.
            </p>
            <i className={`${styles.quoteIcon} bx bxs-quote-alt-left`}></i>
            <div className={styles.details}>
              <span className={styles.name}>Marnie Lotter</span>
              <span className={styles.job}>Web Developer</span>
            </div>
          </SwiperSlide>
        </Swiper>
        <div className={styles.swiperButtonNext}></div>
        <div className={styles.swiperButtonPrev}></div>
        <div className={
          <div className={styles.swiperPagination}></div>
          </div>
        </section>
      );
  };
  
  export default Testimonial;
  
 
import { Swiper, SwiperSlide } from "swiper/react";
import SwiperCore, { Autoplay, Navigation, Pagination } from "swiper";
import "swiper/swiper-bundle.min.css";
import styles from "../styles/Testimonial.module.css";
import Image from "next/image";
import profileImage from "../assets/images/testimonial_image.jpg";
import profileImage1 from "../assets/images/testimonial1_image.jpg";
import profileImage2 from "../assets/images/testimonial2_image.jpg";

SwiperCore.use([Autoplay, Navigation, Pagination]);

const Testimonial = () => {
  return (
    <section className={styles.container}>
      <Swiper
        slidesPerView={1}
        navigation={{
          nextEl: `.${styles.swiperButtonNext}`,
          prevEl: `.${styles.swiperButtonPrev}`,

        pagination={{ clickable: true }}
        autoplay={{ delay: 5000 }}

            eligendi ipsum adipisci, fugit, architecto amet asperiores

            <span className={styles.job}>Web Developer</span>

  width: 40px;
  border-radius: 50%;
  transform: translateY(30px);
  background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.1);
  transition: 0.2s;
  display: flex;
  align-items: center;
  justify-content: center;
  position: absolute;
  top: 50%;
  transform: translateY(-50%);
  z-index: 10;
  cursor: pointer;
}

.swiperButtonNext {
  right: 0;
}

.swiperButtonPrev {
  left: 0;
}

.swiperButtonNext::after,
.swiperButtonNext::before,
.swiperButtonPrev::after,
.swiperButtonPrev::before {
  font-size: 20px;
  color: #fff;
}

.swiperPagination {
  margin-top: 20px;
  display: flex;
  align-items: center;
  justify-content: center;
}

.swiper-pagination-bullet {
  background-color: rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.8);
  width: 10px;
  height: 10px;
  border-radius: 50%;
  margin: 0 5px;
  cursor: pointer;
}

.swiper-pagination-bullet-active {
  background-color: #4070f4;
}

@media screen and (max-width: 768px) {
  .slide {
    padding: 0 20px;
  }
  .swiperButtonNext,
  .swiperButtonPrev {
    display: none;
  }
}

import React, { useRef, useEffect } from "react";
import SwiperCore, { Navigation, Pagination, Autoplay } from "swiper";
import { Swiper, SwiperSlide } from "swiper/react";
import "swiper/swiper-bundle.min.css";
import styles from "../styles/Testimonial.module.css";
import Image from "next/image";
import profileImage from "../assets/images/testimonial_image.jpg";
import profileImage1 from "../assets/images/testimonial1_image.jpg";
import profileImage2 from "../assets/images/testimonial2_image.jpg";

SwiperCore.use([Navigation, Pagination, Autoplay]);

const Testimonial = () => {
  const swiperRef = useRef(null);

  useEffect(() => {
    const swiperInstance = swiperRef.current.swiper;
    const autoplayDelay = 5000; // 5 seconds

    swiperInstance.autoplay.start();
    swiperInstance.autoplay.delay = autoplayDelay;

    return () => {
      swiperInstance.autoplay.stop();
    };
  }, []);

  return (
    <section className={styles.container}>
      <div className={`${styles.testimonial} ${styles.mySwiper}`}>
        <Swiper
          ref={swiperRef}
          spaceBetween={30}
          slidesPerView={1}
          navigation={{
            nextEl: `.${styles.swiperButtonNext}`,
            prevEl: `.${styles.swiperButtonPrev}`,
          }}
          pagination={{ clickable: true, el: `.${styles.swiperPagination}` }}
          autoplay={{ delay: 5000 }}
        >
          <SwiperSlide>
            <div className={styles.slide}>
              <Image src={profileImage} alt="" className={styles.image} />
              <p>
                Lorem ipsum dolor sit amet, consectetur adipisicing elit. Aperiam,
                saepe provident dolorem a quaerat quo error facere nihil deleniti
                eligendi ipsum adipisci, fugit, architecto amet asperiores
                doloremque deserunt eum nemo.
              </p>
              <i className={`${styles.quoteIcon} bx bxs-quote-alt-left`}></i>
              <div className={styles.details}>
                <span className={styles.name}>Marnie Lotter</span>
                <span className={styles.job}>Web Developer</span>
              </div>
            </div>
          </SwiperSlide>
          <SwiperSlide>
            <div className={styles.slide}>
              <Image src={profileImage1} alt="" className={styles.image} />
              <p>
                Lorem ipsum dolor sit amet, consectetur adipisicing elit. Aperiam,
                saepe provident dolorem a quaerat quo error facere nihil deleniti
                eligendi ipsum adipisci, fugit, architecto amet asperiores
                doloremque deserunt eum nemo.
              </p>
              <i className={`${styles.quoteIcon} bx bxs-quote-alt-left`}></i>
              <div className={styles.details}>
                <span className={styles.name}>Marnie Lotter</span>
                <span className={styles.job}>Web Developer</span>
              </div>
            </div>
          </SwiperSlide>
          <SwiperSlide>
            <div className={styles.slide}>
              <Image src={profileImage2} alt="" className={styles.image} />
              <p>
                Lorem ipsum dolor sit amet, consectetur adipisicing elit. Aperiam,
                saepe provident dolorem a quaerat quo error facere nihil deleniti
                eligendi ipsum adipisci, fugit, architecto amet asperiores
                doloremque deserunt eum nemo.
              </p>
              <i className={`${styles.quoteIcon} bx bxs-quote-alt-left`}></i>
              <div className={styles.details}>
                <span className={styles.name}>Marnie Lotter</span>
                <span className={styles.job}>Web Developer</span>
              </div>
            </div>
          </SwiperSlide>
        </Swiper>
        <div className={styles.swiperButtonNext}></div>
        <div className={styles.swiperButtonPrev}></div>
        <div
className={styles.swiperPagination}></div>
</div>
</section>
);
};

export default Testimonial;

            />
          </div>
        </div>
        <div className={styles.textBox}>
          <div className={styles.textContainer}>
            <h2 className={styles.heading}>Welcome to Thapathali Campus</h2>
            <p className={styles.description}>
              I invite you to explore our vibrant and inclusive learning
              environment. With dedicated faculty, cutting-edge facilities, and
              innovative programs, we strive to empower students for success.
              Join us in fostering excellence, diversity, and personal growth.
              Feel free to reach out to us with any questions or inquiries.

Thapathali Campus, located at the center of Kathmandu city, was established in 2023 B.S. (1967 AD) to develop middle-level manpower in the field of mechanical and automobile engineering. It is one of the constituent campuses of the Institute of Engineering under Tribhuvan University, which has upgraded its programs to bachelor and master's level over time.

Apologies for the misalignment. To align the image and text box properly and increase the width of the text box, you can make the following adjustments:

css
Copy code
 
 the parent containers have enough space to accommodate the image and text box widths to avoid overflow issues.


 

.wrapper {
  display: flex;
  flex-direction: column;
  align-items: center;
  padding: 2rem;
}

  }
